  <span id="freeText386584372256598483" style="display:none"><i>Dear Die-ary, I stared, motionless, before the mirror. As always, I stayed until I'm convinced that there is no glass, nothing, separating me from the room I see on the other side. I imagine that everything is different over there. Better. There are people, in that world, who I would like. But, like always, my hand hits the glass. I know that if I'd only waited just one more second... Shit. I'm gonna go kill a party clown.</i><br /><br />Johnnyâcall him Nnyâhas problems. Nobody gets his humor, Mr. Eff and Mr. Z debate over whether Nny should kill himself, callous, self-centered people stand in judgement over others, it's impossible to get a BrainFreezy after 2 AM, the blood on the wall keeps drying out, his Happy Noodle Boy comics depress him, and the girl he liked kicked him in the head and ran away. It's a good thing he has Nail Bunny and his Die-ary to keep him company, not to mention the boy next door that he's got a soft spot for and inadvertently terrifies on a regular basis.<br /><br />A (frequently heavy-handed) screed against judging others by their appearances, Vasquez (best known for <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Invader_Zim" rel="nofollow noopener">Invader Zim</a>), has, in JTHM, created a morbidly hilarious look at life, consumerism, and the worst in all of us. And, of course, Happy Noodle Boy, or, as he might put it, "No! Don't leave me, intestinal gas! Please! Don't go!! I thought you loved me!!" </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9600413-dominique?shelf=villain-protagonist">villain-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9600413-dominique?shelf=own-a-copy">own-a-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9600413-dominique?shelf=gothic">gothic</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666303624" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2412872566180550346">I remember ordering this from Barnes & Noble after re-runs of <i>Invader Zim</i> were coming back to Nicktoons. By then, I became obsessed with the show and this comic seemed interesting to me. At the time, I was a troubled teenager who liked the idea of killing bullies -- I know, twisted, but certainly not to the extent Eric Harris & Dylan Klebold had.<br/>There were only one or two copies at the Barnes & Noble store, and I believe I read just the first quarter of it. After buying it, I read the rest, and </span>
  <span id="freeText2412872566180550346" style="display:none">I remember ordering this from Barnes &amp; Noble after re-runs of <i>Invader Zim</i> were coming back to Nicktoons. By then, I became obsessed with the show and this comic seemed interesting to me. At the time, I was a troubled teenager who liked the idea of killing bullies -- I know, twisted, but certainly not to the extent Eric Harris &amp; Dylan Klebold had.<br />There were only one or two copies at the Barnes &amp; Noble store, and I believe I read just the first quarter of it. After buying it, I read the rest, and really enjoyed it.<br />While it can be disturbing and rude, there were times where I did laugh, such as the author's little commentary. And then there was that shocking mood whiplash, with Johnny <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[wanting to kill himself the first time <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br />What I really love is how there's a slow build-up to the story, what with Johnny's conversations with his two Pillsbury statues and dead bunny. There's all this talk about Johnny's mental state and what's up with his blood-covered wall. Besides black humor, it also has a deep and serious side. I liked and sympathized with the insane main character, and also loved his relationship with his next-door neighbor.<br />Even though it can appear rather messy, I enjoyed Vasquez's art style -- not only because I could see some resemblances to his future characters in <i>Invader Zim</i>, but also because he really put a lot of detail into it, especially <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the monster <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br />The ending was pretty satisfying, too.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2412872566180550346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/850061924" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6162113-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1325312586p2/6162113.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/850061924?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/6162113-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6162113-emily?shelf=recommended">recommended</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850061924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7127070680842637444">Johnny is a criminally insane, introverted young man on a killing spree, his victims being those who taunt and make fun of him, all to feed the red wall with their blood. Driven by the voices in his head projected on to dead bunny, and two styrofoam pigs, he struggles with his madness and the fact that no matter what atrocities he commits, he is never caught.<br/><br/>When my girlfriend recommended this book to me and told me that I'd relate on a scary level, I thought she was exaggerating just a tiny bit</span>
  <span id="freeText7127070680842637444" style="display:none">Johnny is a criminally insane, introverted young man on a killing spree, his victims being those who taunt and make fun of him, all to feed the red wall with their blood. Driven by the voices in his head projected on to dead bunny, and two styrofoam pigs, he struggles with his madness and the fact that no matter what atrocities he commits, he is never caught.<br /><br />When my girlfriend recommended this book to me and told me that I'd relate on a scary level, I thought she was exaggerating just a tiny bit. Sure, I've struggled with mental illness (hearing voices, seeing things, suicidal depression), I'm introverted, I've been bullied, but scarily relate to Nny?..... Well, yes. I really did. By no means do I exaggerate when I say Johnny the Homicidal Maniac is my inner monologue, and I do connect to him on very scary levels. <br /><br />The illustrations in this book are styled much like Jhonen Vasquez's other creation, Invader Zim, which was a huge selling point for me as I love that show. I love the plot of this book, it's not just a bunch of murderous comic strips with a deranged character. The murders mean something, Johnny's struggles and insanity have a point, and the story progresses at a nice pace. It was easy to follow and I had no trouble getting back into the story after setting it down for a while (not that I wanted to). <br /><br />If you're a fan of Invader Zim, the macabre, and insane characters with kick ass boots and a magically changing shirt, then this is definitely the book for you!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7127070680842637444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1229151345" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229151345" />
    <a title="Devin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26092199-devin"><img alt="Devin" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1229151345?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Devin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Devin" href="/user/show/26092199-devin">Devin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26092199-devin?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26092199-devin?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26092199-devin?shelf=comics">comics</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26092199-devin?shelf=collections-and-anthologies">collections-and-anthologies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1229151345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8405277842351754709">I'm only giving this 4 stars instead of 5 because of the fact that the Wobbly Headed Bob comic strips and the Meanwhile comic strips were exempt and instead collected in their respective categories at the end of the collection of Squee's Wonderful Big Giant Book of Unspeakable Horrors. And of course, some of the scenes of the Meanwhile comic strips are referenced later in the Johnny the Homicidal Maniac storyline. I would have preferred having all of the comic shorts included and in their origin</span>
  <span id="freeText8405277842351754709" style="display:none">I'm only giving this 4 stars instead of 5 because of the fact that the Wobbly Headed Bob comic strips and the Meanwhile comic strips were exempt and instead collected in their respective categories at the end of the collection of Squee's Wonderful Big Giant Book of Unspeakable Horrors. And of course, some of the scenes of the Meanwhile comic strips are referenced later in the Johnny the Homicidal Maniac storyline. I would have preferred having all of the comic shorts included and in their original places chronologically as it was originally published. But I do see that Jhonen Vasquez was trying to construct a collection of exclusively Johnny material. Another thing I though was a little disappointing was that the only place where the original covers of each issue are shown are in the issue summaries that are in the extras at the end of the book, and the covers are printed small so you can't see the full awesomeness of them. Squee's graphic novel collection had a similar problem, except that that collection didn't even have an issue-by-issue summary section and so the covers in that book aren't even featured at all. It's only minor things like this that are irritating about this book. Other than that, being able to reread the entire series in one convenient book and seeing all the extras and reading Vasquez's hilarious articles was truly a fantastic experience. If you are a fan of JTHM, this is a must-have!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8405277842351754709" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_367826668" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/367826668" />
    <a title="Jorge Rios" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10877407-jorge-rios"><img alt="Jorge Rios" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1342042545p2/10877407.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/367826668?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jorge Rios" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jorge Rios" href="/user/show/10877407-jorge-rios">Jorge Rios</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10877407-jorge-rios?shelf=graphic-novels-comics">graphic-novels-comics</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10877407-jorge-rios?shelf=comics-graphic-novels">comics-graphic-novels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer367826668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16606143352456036079">What can I say about JTHM? I'll start by clearing a few points. A lot of people will pick this up because of Invader Zim, and I'm pretty sure they'll expect something similar... But alas, it's no Zim. Not that it's bad but Nny certainly requires a more mature audience, the humor still as twisted. I could go on about the plot but I'd rather focus on what you are getting. You get all 7 issues of the JTHM run, sprinkled with a few Meanwhiles, PSA, Happy Noodle Boy (who is like Gir, but more popular</span>
  <span id="freeText16606143352456036079" style="display:none">What can I say about JTHM? I'll start by clearing a few points. A lot of people will pick this up because of Invader Zim, and I'm pretty sure they'll expect something similar... But alas, it's no Zim. Not that it's bad but Nny certainly requires a more mature audience, the humor still as twisted. I could go on about the plot but I'd rather focus on what you are getting. You get all 7 issues of the JTHM run, sprinkled with a few Meanwhiles, PSA, Happy Noodle Boy (who is like Gir, but more popular with hobos) strips etc. It does not contain all the other side comics(Wobbly-headed Bob? Not to be found. :l OR THE CHICKEN F***er) found in the single issues ( but that's just fine, Squee has your back). All the goodies you expect from a Directors Cut... It also allows a glimpse to the more humble beginnings of Nny, showing early drawings, strips from Jhonens HS newspaper. It's an awesome comic but a lot of fans will find the need to own Squee's Wonderful Big Giant Book of Unspeakable Horrors to compliment their collection, and while yo are already at it, I Feel Sick too. The art is awesome and the gore is well... gorey, Jhonen displays his ability to be subtle, brutal...yet classy..(line taken from a friend :P) until you reach Happy Noodle Boy, which a lot of people think is trash (but hey, that was Jhonens goal) but can be seen as Nny's outlet. Overall just an awesome comic to own.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16606143352456036079" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6fUPezbHlzewyV8rkXttY4iigf63jwL+UuX2gogdSWPV7a3OBb9W8ZwkuSaAaCsK9eGHKu0sjsnJEnXOLEqRlw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('g/WHi2s/tCNhV6wcQzsdU6QbhxBDtHAoTSZkI7ad5ge/7SU+WEd15U26ShFSKFs62ViBxBkX/B/W0edvEso+8w==')})
  }
